  <span m='3871040'>to</span> <span m='3871220'>the</span> <span m='3871370'>other</span>
  <span m='3871580'>orbit,</span> <span m='3872380'>searches</span> <span m='3872900'>for</span>
  <span m='3873020'>the</span> <span m='3873140'>target,</span> <span m='3873620'>identifies</span>
  <span m='3874370'>it</span> <span m='3874580'>rendezvous</span> <span m='3875120'>and</span>
  <span m='3875240'>approach,</span> <span m='3875720'>docking</span> <span m='3876110'>and</span>
  <span m='3876200'>capture,</span> <span m='3877520'>does</span> <span m='3877750'>an</span>
  <span m='3877880'>orbital</span> <span m='3878330'>transfer</span> <span m='3879410'>and</span>
  <span m='3879500'>then</span> <span m='3879620'>releases</span> <span m='3880280'>the</span>
  <span m='3880700'>target</span> <span m='3881090'>satellite</span> <span m='3881720'>at</span>

  <span m='3883070'>verifies</span> <span m='3883660'>its</span> <span m='3883780'>status</span>
  <span m='3884510'>and</span> <span m='3884630'>then</span> <span m='3884810'>either</span>

  </p><p><span m='3889040'>And</span> <span m='3889340'>as</span> <span m='3889490'>you</span>

  <span m='3893390'>expensive.</span> <span m='3894920'>It's</span> <span m='3895130'>less</span>

  <span m='4059860'>step</span> <span m='4060220'>curve</span> <span m='4060640'>because</span>

  <span m='4063970'>can</span> <span m='4064090'>now</span> <span m='4064330'>operate</span>

  <span m='4066070'>regime.</span> </p><p><span m='4068360'>The</span> <span m='4069020'>capability.</span>
  <span m='4069890'>The</span> <span m='4070010'>payload</span> <span m='4070490'>mass</span>

  <span m='4073460'>discretized</span> <span m='4074240'>between</span> <span m='4074600'>low,</span>

  <span m='4094780'>V</span> <span m='4095210'>60%,</span> <span m='4096189'>and</span>

  <span m='4101960'>that</span> <span m='4102170'>important</span> <span m='4102770'>compared</span>

  <span m='4108680'>of</span> <span m='4109060'>the</span> <span m='4109160'>calculations.</span>
  <span m='4110689'>That's</span> <span m='4110899'>in</span> <span m='4111050'>that</span>
  <span m='4111170'>paper,</span> <span m='4111779'>which</span> <span m='4111890'>I'll</span>
  <span m='4112040'>post.</span> <span m='4113920'>You</span> <span m='4114050'>get</span>
  <span m='4114290'>this.</span> <span m='4115920'>So</span> <span m='4115939'>this</span>
  <span m='4116120'>is</span> <span m='4116240'>a</span> <span m='4116300'>cloud</span>
